## Idea

## Definitions

### The standard definition of multiplication on ℤ

<pre class="Agda"><a id="mul-ℤ"></a><a id="2230" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2238" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a> <a id="2240" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2242" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a> <a id="2244" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2246" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a>
<a id="2248" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2254" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2255" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="2259" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1551" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a><a id="2265" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2267" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2267" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="2269" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2271" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#3916" class="Function">neg-ℤ</a> <a id="2277" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2267" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="2279" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2285" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2286" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="2290" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2291" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="2298" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2298" class="Bound">x</a><a id="2299" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="2302" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2302" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="2304" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2306" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#1505" class="Function">add-ℤ</a> <a id="2312" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2313" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#3916" class="Function">neg-ℤ</a> <a id="2319" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2302" class="Bound">l</a><a id="2320" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2322" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2323" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2329" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2330" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="2334" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2298" class="Bound">x</a><a id="2335" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2337" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2302" class="Bound">l</a><a id="2338" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="2340" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2346" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2347" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="2351" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2352" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="2356" href="foundation.unit-type.html#1108" class="InductiveConstructor">star</a><a id="2360" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="2363" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2363" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="2365" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2367" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2150" class="Function">zero-ℤ</a>
<a id="2374" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2380" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2381" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="2385" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2386" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="2390" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1551" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a><a id="2396" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="2399" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2399" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="2401" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2403" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2399" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="2405" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2411" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2412" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="2416" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2417" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="2421" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2422" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="2429" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2429" class="Bound">x</a><a id="2430" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="2434" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2434" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="2436" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2438" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#1505" class="Function">add-ℤ</a> <a id="2444" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2434" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="2446" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2447" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2453" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2454" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="2458" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2459" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="2463" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2429" class="Bound">x</a><a id="2464" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="2467" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2434" class="Bound">l</a><a id="2468" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="mul-ℤ&#39;"></a><a id="2471" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2471" class="Function">mul-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="2478" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2480" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a> <a id="2482" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2484" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a> <a id="2486" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2488" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a>
<a id="2490" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2471" class="Function">mul-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="2497" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2497" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2499" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2499" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2501" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2503" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2509" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2499" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2511" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2497" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="ap-mul-ℤ"></a><a id="2514" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2514" class="Function">ap-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2523" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="2527" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2528" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2528" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2530" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2530" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2532" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2532" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="2535" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2535" class="Bound">y&#39;</a> <a id="2538" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2540" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="2541" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2543" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2545" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2528" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2547" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="2549" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2532" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="2552" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2554" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2530" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2556" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="2558" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2535" class="Bound">y&#39;</a> <a id="2561" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2563" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2569" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2528" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2571" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2530" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2573" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="2575" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2581" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2532" class="Bound">x&#39;</a> <a id="2584" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2535" class="Bound">y&#39;</a>
<a id="2587" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2514" class="Function">ap-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2596" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2596" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="2598" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2598" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="2600" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2602" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#7450" class="Function">ap-binary</a> <a id="2612" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="2618" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2596" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="2620" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2598" class="Bound">q</a>
</pre>
### A definition of multiplication that connects with multiplication on ℕ

## Properties

### Laws for multiplication on ℤ

<pre class="Agda"><a id="left-zero-law-mul-ℤ"></a><a id="3455" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#3455" class="Function">left-zero-law-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="3475" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3477" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3478" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#3478" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3480" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3482" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="3483" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3485" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3487" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="3493" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2150" class="Function">zero-ℤ</a> <a id="3500" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#3478" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3502" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="3504" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2150" class="Function">zero-ℤ</a>
<a id="3511" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#3455" class="Function">left-zero-law-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="3531" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#3531" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3533" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3535" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1820" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

<a id="right-zero-law-mul-ℤ"></a><a id="3541" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#3541" class="Function">right-zero-law-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="3562" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3565" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#3565" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3567" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3569" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="3570" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3572" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3574" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="3580" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#3565" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="3582" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2150" class="Function">zero-ℤ</a> <a id="3589" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="3591" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2150" class="Function">zero-ℤ</a>
<a id="3598" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#3541" class="Function">right-zero-law-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="3619" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3620" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="3624" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1551" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a><a id="3630" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3632" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3634" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1820" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

### Positivity of multiplication

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-positive-mul-ℤ"></a><a id="13554" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13554" class="Function">is-positive-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="13572" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="13576" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13577" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13577" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13579" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13579" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13581" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13583" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="13584" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13586" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13588" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#7414" class="Function">is-positive-ℤ</a> <a id="13602" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13577" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13604" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13606" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#7414" class="Function">is-positive-ℤ</a> <a id="13620" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13579" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13622" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13624" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#7414" class="Function">is-positive-ℤ</a> <a id="13638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13639" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="13645" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13577" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13647" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13579" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13648" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="13650" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13554" class="Function">is-positive-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="13668" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13669" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13673" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13674" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13678" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1551" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a><a id="13684" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13687" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13688" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13692" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13693" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13697" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13697" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13698" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13701" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13701" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="13703" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13703" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="13705" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13707" href="foundation.unit-type.html#1108" class="InductiveConstructor">star</a>
<a id="13712" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13554" class="Function">is-positive-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="13730" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13731" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13735" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13736" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13740" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13741" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="13748" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13748" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13749" class="Symbol">))}</a> <a id="13753" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13754" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13758" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13759" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13763" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13763" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13764" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13767" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13767" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="13769" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13769" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="13771" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="13775" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#12181" class="Function">is-positive-add-ℤ</a> <a id="13793" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13794" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13798" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13799" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13803" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13763" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13804" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13807" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13769" class="Bound">K</a>
    <a id="13813" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13815" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13554" class="Function">is-positive-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="13833" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13834" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13838" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13839" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13843" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13748" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13844" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13847" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13848" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13852" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13853" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="13857" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13763" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13858" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13861" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13767" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="13863" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13769" class="Bound">K</a><a id="13864" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Computing multiplication of integers that come from natural numbers

<pre class="Agda"><a id="mul-int-ℕ"></a><a id="13952" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13952" class="Function">mul-int-ℕ</a> <a id="13962" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13964" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13965" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13965" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13967" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13967" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13969" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13971" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1530" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="13972" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13974" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13976" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="13982" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13983" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="13989" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13965" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13990" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13992" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13993" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="13999" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13967" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14000" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14002" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="14004" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="14010" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14011" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1286" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="14017" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13965" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14019" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13967" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14020" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="14022" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13952" class="Function">mul-int-ℕ</a> <a id="14032" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1551" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a> <a id="14039" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14039" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="14041" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14043" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1820" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
<a id="14048" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13952" class="Function">mul-int-ℕ</a> <a id="14058" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14059" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="14066" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14066" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14067" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14069" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14069" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="14071" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="14075" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14077" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="14080" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14081" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2471" class="Function">mul-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="14088" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14089" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="14095" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14069" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14096" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14099" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14100" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="14104" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14105" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#10842" class="Function">succ-int-ℕ</a> <a id="14116" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14066" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14117" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="14121" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="14125" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14127" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14129" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#4870" class="Function">left-successor-law-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="14154" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14155" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="14161" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14066" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14162" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14164" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14165" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="14171" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14069" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14172" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14175" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
    <a id="14181" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14183" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14185" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14187" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="14190" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14191" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#1505" class="Function">add-ℤ</a> <a id="14197" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14198" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="14204" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14069" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14205" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14208" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14209" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#13952" class="Function">mul-int-ℕ</a> <a id="14219" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14066" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14221" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14069" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14222" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14225" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
        <a id="14235" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14237" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#12585" class="Function">add-int-ℕ</a> <a id="14247" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14069" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="14249" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14250" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1286" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="14256" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14066" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14258" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14069" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14259" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="14263" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
      <a id="14271" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14273" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="14276" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="14282" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14283" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#2172" class="Function">commutative-add-ℕ</a> <a id="14301" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14069" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="14303" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14304" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1286" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="14310" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14066" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14312" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14069" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14313" class="Symbol">)))))</a>

<a id="compute-mul-ℤ"></a><a id="14320" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14320" class="Function">compute-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="14334" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14336" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14337" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14337" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14339" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14339" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="14341" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14343" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="14344" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14346" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14348" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="14354" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14337" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14356" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14339" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="14358" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="14360" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2710" class="Function">explicit-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="14375" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14337" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14377" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14339" class="Bound">y</a>
<a id="14379" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14320" class="Function">compute-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="14393" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14394" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="14398" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1551" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a><a id="14404" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14406" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14407" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="14411" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14411" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14412" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14414" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="14418" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="14422" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14423" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="14426" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="14432" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14433" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#2195" class="Function">left-unit-law-mul-ℕ</a> <a id="14453" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14454" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="14461" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14411" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14462" class="Symbol">)))</a>
<a id="14466" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14320" class="Function">compute-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="14480" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14481" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="14485" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14486" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="14493" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14493" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14494" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14497" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14498" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="14502" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14502" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14503" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14505" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="14509" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14511" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14513" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="14516" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14517" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#1505" class="Function">add-ℤ</a> <a id="14523" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14524" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="14530" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14531" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="14538" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14502" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14539" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="14543" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14544" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14320" class="Function">compute-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="14558" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14559" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="14563" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14493" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14564" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14566" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14567" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="14571" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14502" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14572" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="14576" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
    <a id="14582" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14584" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#6403" class="Function">commutative-add-ℤ</a>
      <a id="14608" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14610" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="14616" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14617" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="14624" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14502" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14625" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="14634" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14636" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="14642" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14643" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1286" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="14649" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14650" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="14657" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14493" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14658" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14661" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="14668" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14502" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14669" class="Symbol">)))))</a> <a id="14675" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>

    <a id="15961" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15963" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="15966" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1250" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="15970" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15971" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#2172" class="Function">commutative-add-ℕ</a> <a id="15989" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#15547" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="15991" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15992" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1286" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="15998" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15999" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16006" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#15537" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16007" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16009" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16010" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16017" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#15547" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16018" class="Symbol">)))))</a>

     <a id="16362" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16364" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a>
       <a id="16375" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16377" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16379" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="16382" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16383" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1169" class="Function">add-ℕ&#39;</a> <a id="16390" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16333" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16391" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16393" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16394" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1721" class="Function">left-zero-law-mul-ℕ</a> <a id="16414" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16415" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16422" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16333" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16423" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="16427" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
         <a id="16438" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16440" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1464" class="Function">left-unit-law-add-ℕ</a> <a id="16460" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16333" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16461" class="Symbol">)))</a>
<a id="16465" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14320" class="Function">compute-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="16479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16480" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="16484" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16485" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="16489" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16490" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16497" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16497" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16498" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="16502" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16503" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="16507" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16508" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="16512" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16512" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16513" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="16516" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="16520" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16522" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="16525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16526" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#1505" class="Function">add-ℤ</a> <a id="16532" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16533" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="16537" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16538" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="16542" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16512" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16543" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="16547" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16548" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#14320" class="Function">compute-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="16562" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16563" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="16567" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16568" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="16572" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16497" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16573" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="16576" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16577" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="16581" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16582" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="16586" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16512" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16587" class="Symbol">))))</a> <a id="16592" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="16596" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16598" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16600" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#12585" class="Function">add-int-ℕ</a> <a id="16610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16611" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16618" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16512" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16619" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16621" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16622" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1286" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="16628" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16629" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16636" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16497" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16637" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16639" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16640" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16647" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16512" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16648" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="16652" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
    <a id="16658" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16660" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="16663" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2525" class="Function">int-ℕ</a> <a id="16669" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16670" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#2172" class="Function">commutative-add-ℕ</a> <a id="16688" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16689" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16696" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16512" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16697" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16700" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1286" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="16706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16707" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16714" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16497" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16715" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16717" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16718" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="16725" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16512" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16726" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
</pre>
### Linearity of the difference

<pre class="Agda"><a id="linear-diff-ℤ"></a><a id="16778" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16778" class="Function">linear-diff-ℤ</a> <a id="16792" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="16796" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16797" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16797" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="16799" id="16803" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16805" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="16806" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16808" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16810" href="elementary-number-theory.difference-integers.html#1194" class="Function">diff-ℤ</a> <a id="16817" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16818" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="16824" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16797" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="16826" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16799" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16827" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16829" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16830" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="16836" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16797" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="16838" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16801" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16839" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16841" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="16843" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="16849"   <a id="16888" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16890" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="16893" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16894" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#1505" class="Function">add-ℤ</a> <a id="16900" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16901" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="16907" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16878" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="16909" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16880" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16910" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="16913" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16914" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="16918" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16919" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#12859" class="Function">right-negative-law-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="16944" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16878" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="16946" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16882" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16947" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="16951" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="16955" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16957" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="16961" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16962" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#12575" class="Function">left-distributive-mul-add-ℤ</a> <a id="16990" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16878" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="16992" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16880" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16994" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16995" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#3916" class="Function">neg-ℤ</a> <a id="17001" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16882" class="Bound">y</a><a id="17002" class="Symbol">)))</a>

<a id="linear-diff-ℤ&#39;"></a><a id="17007" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17007" class="Function">linear-diff-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="17022" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="17026" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17027" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17027" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17029" id="17056" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17031" class="Bound">z</a><a id="17057" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17059" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17060" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="17066" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17029" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="17068" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17031" class="Bound">z</a><a id="17069" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17071" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1865" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="17073" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="17079" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17080" href="elementary-number-theory.difference-integers.html#1194" class="Function">diff-ℤ</a> <a id="17087" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17027" class="Bound">x</a> <a href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17031" class="Bound">z</a>
<a id="17094" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17007" class="Function">linear-diff-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="17109" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17109" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17111" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17111" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="17113" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17113" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="17115" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="17119" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17121" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="17124" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17125" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-integers.html#1505" class="Function">add-ℤ</a> <a id="17131" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17132" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="17138" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17109" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17140" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17113" class="Bound">z</a><a id="17141" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="17144" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17145" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="17149" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17150" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#10574" class="Function">left-negative-law-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="17174" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17111" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="17176" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17113" class="Bound">z</a><a id="17177" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="17181" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
  <a id="17185" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17187" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="17191" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17192" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#9607" class="Function">right-distributive-mul-add-ℤ</a> <a id="17221" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17109" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17223" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17224" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#3916" class="Function">neg-ℤ</a> <a id="17230" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17111" class="Bound">y</a><a id="17231" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17233" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17113" class="Bound">z</a><a id="17234" class="Symbol">))</a>

### Injectivity of multiplication

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-injective-mul-ℤ"></a><a id="18038" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18038" class="Function">is-injective-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18057" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="18061" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18062" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18062" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18064" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18066" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="18067" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18069" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18071" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2239" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℤ</a> <a id="18084" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18062" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18086" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18088" href="foundation.injective-maps.html#1309" class="Function">is-injective</a> <a id="18101" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18102" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18108" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18062" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18109" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="18111" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18038" class="Function">is-injective-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18130" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18130" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18132" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18132" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18134" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18135" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18135" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18136" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18138" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18139" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18139" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18140" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18142" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18142" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="18144" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="18148" href="elementary-number-theory.difference-integers.html#1357" class="Function">eq-diff-ℤ</a>
    <a id="18162" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18164" href="foundation.type-arithmetic-empty-type.html#4655" class="Function">map-left-unit-law-coprod-is-empty</a>
      <a id="18204" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18206" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2186" class="Function">is-zero-ℤ</a> <a id="18216" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18130" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18217" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="18225" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18227" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2186" class="Function">is-zero-ℤ</a> <a id="18237" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18238" href="elementary-number-theory.difference-integers.html#1194" class="Function">diff-ℤ</a> <a id="18245" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18135" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18247" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18139" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18248" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="18257" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18259" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18132" class="Bound">f</a><a id="18260" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="18268" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18270" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#17250" class="Function">is-zero-is-zero-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18292" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18130" class="Bound">x</a>
        <a id="18302" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18304" href="elementary-number-theory.difference-integers.html#1194" class="Function">diff-ℤ</a> <a id="18311" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18135" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18313" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18139" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18314" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="18324" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18326" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="18330" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18331" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#16778" class="Function">linear-diff-ℤ</a> <a id="18345" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18130" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18347" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18135" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18349" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18139" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18350" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18352" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="18354" href="elementary-number-theory.difference-integers.html#1738" class="Function">is-zero-diff-ℤ</a> <a id="18369" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18142" class="Bound">p</a><a id="18370" class="Symbol">)))</a>

<a id="is-injective-mul-ℤ&#39;"></a><a id="18375" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18375" class="Function">is-injective-mul-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="18395" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="18399" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18400" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18400" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18402" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18404" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="18405" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18407" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18409" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2239" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℤ</a> <a id="18422" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18400" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18424" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18426" href="foundation.injective-maps.html#1309" class="Function">is-injective</a> <a id="18439" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18440" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2471" class="Function">mul-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="18447" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18400" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18448" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="18450" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18375" class="Function">is-injective-mul-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="18470" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18470" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18472" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18472" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18474" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18475" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18475" class="Bound">y</a><a id="18476" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18478" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18479" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18479" class="Bound">z</a><a id="18480" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18482" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18482" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="18484" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="18488" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18038" class="Function">is-injective-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18507" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18470" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18509" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18472" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18511" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18512" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#12015" class="Function">commutative-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18530" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18470" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18532" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18475" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="18534" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="18536" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18537" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18482" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="18539" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="18541" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#12015" class="Function">commutative-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18559" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18479" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="18561" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18470" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18562" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### Multiplication by a nonzero integer is an embedding

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-emb-mul-ℤ"></a><a id="18635" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18635" class="Function">is-emb-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18648" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18650" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18651" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18651" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18653" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18655" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="18656" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18658" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18660" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#2239" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℤ</a> <a id="18673" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18651" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18675" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18677" href="foundation-core.embeddings.html#992" class="Function">is-emb</a> <a id="18684" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18685" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18691" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18651" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18692" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="18694" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18635" class="Function">is-emb-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18707" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18707" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18709" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18709" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18711" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18713" href="foundation.injective-maps.html#4586" class="Function">is-emb-is-injective</a> <a id="18733" href="elementary-number-theory.equality-integers.html#3315" class="Function">is-set-ℤ</a> <a id="18742" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18743" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18038" class="Function">is-injective-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="18762" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18707" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18764" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#18709" class="Bound">f</a><a id="18765" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="19569" class="Comment">-- Lemmas about nonnegative integers</a>

<a id="is-nonnegative-mul-ℤ"></a><a id="19607" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#19607" class="Function">is-nonnegative-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="19628" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="19632" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19633" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#19633" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19635" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#19635" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="19637" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19639" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#1907" class="Function">ℤ</a><a id="19640" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19642" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19644" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#6828" class="Function">is-nonnegative-ℤ</a> <a id="19661" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#19633" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19663" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19665" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#6828" class="Function">is-nonnegative-ℤ</a> <a id="19682" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#19635" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="19684" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="19688" href="elementary-number-theory.integers.html#6828" class="Function">is-nonnegative-ℤ</a> <a id="19705" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19706" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#2230" class="Function">mul-ℤ</a> <a id="19712" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#19633" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19714" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#19635" class="Bound">y</a><a id="19715" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="20979" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20981" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#20612" class="Function">preserves-leq-mul-ℤ</a> <a id="21001" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#20842" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21003" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#20844" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="21005" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21006" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="21010" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21011" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1268" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="21015" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#20864" class="Bound">n</a><a id="21016" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="21019" href="foundation.unit-type.html#1108" class="InductiveConstructor">star</a> <a id="21024" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#20874" class="Bound">K</a><a id="21025" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="preserves-leq-mul-ℤ&#39;"></a><a id="21028" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#21028" class="Function">preserves-leq-mul-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="21049" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="21130" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#21028" class="Function">preserves-leq-mul-ℤ&#39;</a> <a id="21151" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#21151" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21153" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#21153" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="21155" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#21155" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="21157" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#21157" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="21159" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-integers.html#21159" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="21161" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="21165" href="elementary-number-theory.inequality-integers.html#2380" class="Function">concatenate-eq-leq-eq-ℤ</a>
